(If the photo shown does not match the one shown on the front of the actual card, it has probably been tampered with and may be a fake card.);\r\n5.\tTouch the Card Details tab to view the list of current qualifications.\r\n6.\tDo the same with more smartcards if you need to.\r\n\r\n\r\nTo read a virtual smartcard:\r\n\r\n1.\tOpen the app;\r\n2.\tTouch the 'SCAN A QR CODE' button;\r\n3.\tRead the QR code (from approx. 10cm away);\r\n4.\tAn image of the card appears. (If the photo shown does not match the one on the cardholder’s phone, it is a fake card.);\r\n5.\tTouch the card image to view the back of the card;\r\n6.\tTouch the Core Data tab to view
